When I opened the door, I was amazed by the view of the 270-degree floor-to-ceiling window. The room can see the beautiful scenery of the entire Lancang River. From time to time, there are yachts flying by. Staying in the room can also look out the window and feel very relaxed.

No one will refuse Xishuangbanna in spring! Wake up in the morning and enjoy breakfast. Put on a swimsuit, put on flip-flops, and jump into the pool. It's really satisfying! A good mood to start the day.

I really like the infinity pool with a river view of the Lancang River. The constant temperature swimming pool, the water temperature is just right, (the water is also very clean, divided into shallow water/deep water areas) The moment when the floating afternoon tea is placed on the transparent swimming pool. It feels like traveling to Bali. You can take blockbusters at will!

The first river view infinity pool hotel in Xishuangbanna. This hotel has a strong sense of design and is suitable for the aesthetics of our young people. The breakfast is also very good, with many varieties, including Dai-style snacks, and delicious beef rice noodles and noodles. You can taste them without leaving the hotel~

The room I chose is a suite, which is said to be more than 90 square meters, which is really big, with a super large balcony with river views, and a 270-degree river view bathtub. The room comes with welcome fruit, cold tea, biscuits, and drinks. The welcome fruit is delicious, and the Southeast Asian snacks are great.

The unlimited number of sightseeing buses in Gaozhuang for free pick-up (at the hotel entrance) is really convenient, and there is also a shuttle bus to pick up at any time until 01:00 in the morning. It is so comfortable not to have to walk back to the hotel after the massage. I love this~

Smart equipment Hansgrohe bathroom, smart toilet-Duravit, one-to-one butler service (Haidilao-style service).

There are Manting Park and Xingguang Night Market nearby. It only takes 10 minutes to walk to Xingguang Night Market, or you can take a sightseeing bus for free pick-up. Unlimited number of people for breakfast (negative 1 floor).
